1PH01     IKFCBL01                                                                                              PAGE    7
-  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                       ASM 0201 11.03 02/14/15
0                                    219+*
                                     220+*TITLE:
                                     221+*
                                     222+*        'IKFCBL01'
                                     223+*
                                     224+*STATUS:
                                     225+*   CHANGE LEVEL 000
                                     226+*
                                     227+*FUNCTION/OPERATION:
                                     228+*
                                     229+*   PERFORMS COMPILER INITIALIZATION.  DETERMINES BUFFER AREA.
                                     230+*   PROCESSES THE EXEC CARD OR THE CALL, LINK, XCTL OR ATTACH MACRO
                                     231+*     COMPILATION PARAMETERS.  OBTAINS STORAGES FOR TABLES, THE
                                     232+*   DICTIONARY AND THE BUFFERS.
                                     233+*   PERFORMS THE BASIS AND COPY FUNCTIONS.
                                     234+*
                                     235+*ENTRY POINTS:
                                     236+*
                                     237+*        'IKFCBL01'
                                     238+*
                                     239+*INPUT - INTERNAL:
                                     240+*
                                     241+*        COMPILATION PARAMETERS FROM PHASE 00
                                     242+*
                                     243+*INPUT - EXTERNAL:
                                     244+*   (ONLY FOR BASIS AND COPY FUNCTIONS)
                                     245+*   SYSIN - SOURCE PROGRAM
                                     246+*   SYSLIB - SOURCE PROGRAM
                                     247+*
                                     248+*OUTPUT - INTERNAL:
                                     249+*
                                     250+*   MODIFIED DCB
                                     251+*   SWITCH INDICATING THE COMPILATION OPTIONS
                                     252+*   LINE COUNT INDICATION
                                     253+*   INDICATION OF DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THA MAX AMOUNT OF CORE STORAGE
                                     254+*   REQUESTED AND THE AMOUNT ACTUALLY RECEIVED FOR TABLES, DICTIONA
                                     255+*   AND BUFFERS.
                                     256+*   BUFFERS ADDRESSES AND LENGTHS
                                     257+*   SYSUT3  E-TEXT FOR BASIS AND COPY STATEMENTS
                                     258+*   SYSUT4  SOURCE PROGRAM FOR PHASE 1 SCAN IF LIB OPTION
                                     259+*           IS IN EFFECT
                                     260+*
                                     261+*OUTPUT - EXTERNAL:
                                     262+*
                                     263+*   SYSPRINT  SOURCE PROGRAM LISTING (IF LIB OPTION IS IN EFFECT)
                                     264+*
                                     265+*EXTERNAL ROUTINES:
                                     266+*
                                     267+*   PHASE 00  LINK TO I-O AND INTERPHASE COMMON REGION
                                     268+*   PRIME  ASSIGN AN AREA IN A TABLE REGION
                                     269+*   TAMEIN  TAMER INITIALIZATION ROUTINE
                                     270+*   INSERT  GET ROOM FOR AN ENTRY IN A TABLE
                                     271+*   TABREL  RELEASE TABLE, FREE AREA IF NO LONGER NEEDED
                                     272+*   STATIC  NOTE NO NEW ENTRY TO BE MADE
                                     273+*
1PH01     IKFCBL01                                                                                              PAGE    8
-  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                       ASM 0201 11.03 02/14/15
0                                    274+*EXITS NORMAL:
                                     275+*
                                     276+*   RETURNS TO PHASE 00
                                     277+*
                                     278+*EXISTS - ERROR:
                                     279+*
                                     280+*   RETURN TO PHASE 00
                                     281+*TABLE/WORK AREAS:
                                     282+*
                                     283+*   REPTAB (REPLACING TABLE) FOR THE COPY FUNCTION
                                     284+*        WITH THE REPLACING OPTION
                                     285+*
                                     286+*ATTRIBUTES:
                                     287+*
                                     288+*   NOT REUSABLE
                                     289+*
                                     290+*NOTES:
                                     291+*
                                     292+*   GENERAL ORGANIZATION:
                                     293+*   1.   EQU'S
                                     294+*   2.   CONSTANTS
                                     295+*   3.   PHASE 01 HOUSEKEEPING AND INITIALIZATION
                                     296+*   4.   SUBROUTINES
                                     297+*   5.   BASIS AND COPY ROUTINES
                                     298+*
                                     299+*
                                     300+*   GENERAL CONSIDERATION IN PHASE 01:
                                     301+*   PHASE 01 IS LOGICALLY A SUBSET OF PHASE 00, BUT IT IS A SEPARAT
                                     302+*   LOAD MODULE, SINCE IT IS NOT NEEDED IN CORE STORAGE THROUGHOUT
                                     303+*   COMPILATION.
                                     304+*
                                     305+*
                                     306+*   THE BUFFER AND TAMER TABLES ARE DESCRIBED IN DETAIL IN PLM
                                     307+*   AND LISTING.
                                     308+*
                                     309+*
                                     310+*

                                    3052+*  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE GETS CONTROL WHEN WE HAVE REACHED THE END

                                    3055+*  EITHER CONTINUED OR IT ENDS IN COL 72, IN THIS CASE THE NEXT TO
                                    3056+*  LAST WORD IS PROCESSED. SINCE THE INPUT PTR IS PAST COL 72, THE

                                    3058+*  PROCESSED.

0                                   3197+****                          INTERPRETIVE STRINGS                 ****
                                    3198+*
                                    3199+*                   EACH ENTRY IS MADE UP OF 1 TO 6 BYTES
                                    3200+*                   WHICH LOOK AS FOLLOWS
                                    3201+*
                                    3202+*                   / 1   / 2   / 3 4   / 5   / 6   /
                                    3203+*                  /X'JK'/X'LL'/X'MNNN'/X'PP'/X'QQ'/
                                    3204+*
                                    3205+*                   WHERE
                                    3206+*                   J = DISPLACEMENT INTO TESTTAB -LIST OF ROUTINES
                                    3207+*                       WHICH DO TESTS ON WORDS
                                    3208+*                   K = DISPLACEMENT INTO CONNECTOR TABLE (CONTAB)
                                    3209+*                       IF TEST PROVES FALSE, CONTAB ADDRESS
                                    3210+*                       DETERMINES WHETHER ALLOWABLE AND WHERE TO GO
                                    3211+*                       TO DO THE SYSTEM ACTION ROUTINE
                                    3212+*                       THIS HALFBYTE HAS SPECIAL MEANING FOR THE
                                    3213+*                       CHANGE-STRING-POINTER ROUTINE (J = 3)
                                    3214+*                   LL = DISPLACEMENT INTO ACTION TABLE (ACTTAB)
                                    3215+*                       IF TEST IS TRUE, ACTTAB GIVES ADDRESS OF
                                    3216+*                       ROUTINE TO BRANCH TO
                                    3217+*                   (MNNN ARE OPTIONAL BYTES, MISSING IF TEST IS NOT
                                    3218+*                   FOR A RESERVED WORD)
                                    3219+*                   M = LENGTH OF WORD (2 THRU F)
                                    3220+*                  NNN= DISPLACEMENT INTO RESERVED WORD LIST FOR
                                    3221+*                       COMPARE OF CURRENT WORD
                                    3222+*                   PP= IF NON ZERO IT IS POINTER TO NEXT STRING
                                    3223+*                       IF ZERO, USE NEXT STRING IN LINE
                                    3224+*                   (QQ IS AN OPTIONAL BYTE, MISSING IF FAILURE TO
                                    3225+*                    SATISFY THE TEST DOES NOT CONSTITUTE AN ERROR
                                    3226+*                    FOR A COPY STATEMENT)
                                    3227+*                   QQ= ERROR BYTE WHICH CONTAINS THE MESSAGE NUMBER
                                    3228+*                       FOR DIAGNOSTICS IF THE TEST ROUTINE WAS NOT
                                    3229+*                       SATISFIED
                                    3230+*
                                    3231+*                   THE CHANGE-STRING-POINTER ROUTINE IS A ONE
                                    3232+*                   BYTE ENTRY
                                    3233+*
                                    3234+*                   REFERENCE TO THE LAST STRING LABEL MUST NOT
                                    3235+*                   EXCEED X'FF' SINCE PP= 1-BYTE.IF THE STRING GROWS
                                    3236+*                   SUCH THAT A POINTER TO THE LAST LABEL EXCEEDS
                                    3237+*                   X'FF', A SPLITTING OF THE STRING IS NECESSARY.
                                    3238+*                   THIS REQUIRES A CHANGE TO THE CALCACT4 ROUTINE
                                    3239+*                   WHICH GETS THE BEGINNING OF THE CURRENT STRING
                                    3240+*                   TO DETERMINE WHICH ENTRY TO BRANCH TO WITHIN
                                    3241+*                   THE STRING. ALSO THE STRING WITHIN WHICH
                                    3242+*                   PROCESSING IS TAKING PLACE AT ANY TIME, SHOULD
                                    3243+*                   HAVE HAD ITS BEGINNING ADDRESS SAVED IN ORDER
                                    3244+*                   TO REFERENCE ANY LABELS WITHIN THAT STRING
                                    3245+***********************************************************************

0                                   3505+***********************************************************************
                                    3506+*
                                    3507+*                        DIAGNOSTIC ROUTINE
                                    3508+*
                                    3509+*        CALLED AS FOLLOWS:
                                    3510+*              BAL L1,DIAGNOSE
                                    3511+*              DC  X'AB'      WHERE A=0 FOR W-LEVEL  B=0 FOR NO INSERT
                                    3512+*              DC  X'YY'              1 FOR C-LEVEL    1 FOR 1  INSERT
                                    3513+*                                     2 FOR E-LEVEL    2 FOR CARD IMAGE
                                    3514+*                                                            INSERT
                                    3515+*                                                      4 FOR 2 INSERTS
                                    3516+*                             YY=MESSAGE NUMBER
                                    3517+*        MESSAGES AND PARAMETERS ARE WRITTEN VIA:
                                    3518+*              LA   C2,ADDRESS-OF-RECORD
                                    3519+*              BALR C0,C5     WHERE C5= A(COS)
                                    3520+*              DC   X'23'     WRITE ON FILE 3
                                    3521+*
                                    3522+*        RETURN TO CALLING ROUTINE VIA L1 REGISTER
                                    3523+*
                                    3524+***********************************************************************
